                                    </list>
                                    <p>Verse SS.6.1.26 and 27 are not in sequence and mixed up with
                                        each other. Folio no 353r has a few words in the margin
                                        below which I couldn’t find where to add them.</p>
                                </note>
                                <note resp="Madhududan Rimal"> 6.41 from NAK 5-333: the ending of
                                    the chapter is: uttaratantre śoṣacikitsā aṣṭatriṃsattamaḥ
                                    kāyacikitsāyāṃ tṛtīyodhyāyaḥ || So it looks like it is being
                                    called chapter 38, not 41. </note>
                                <note resp="Vandana Lele">

                                <note resp="Vandana Lele">
                                    <list>
                                        <item>1) I have doubt about the chapter number as the
                                            colophon of the manuscript mentions:
                                            "uttaratantre'ṣṭapañcāśattamaḥ kāyacikitsāyāṃ
                                            yonivyāpaccikitsā trayoviṅśatitamo'dhyāyaḥ samāptaḥ ||"
                                            As I have understood it, the above heading is given to
                                            the subject of this mail . I have also marked the same
                                            in the transcription file. Please comment.</item>
                                        <item>2) The folios which I have transcribed i.e 480r:3,
                                            480v, 481r, 481v are not paginated.</item>
                                        <item>3) Missing verses: 6.38.2, 3, 4, 5ab, 5cd, 5, 6, 7,
                                            6.38.30ab, 32cd, 32ef Probably, 6.38.4.1 is left out to
                                            mark in the vulgate copy, like other verses 6.38.3.1,
                                            6.38.2 etc. which are in manuscript. I am not sure about
                                            this observation. In vulgate, verse number 6.38.8.1 is
                                            shown as missing but in manuscript I could not find
                                            different text relating to that for addition. (Here,
                                            also I may be wrong.)</item>
                                        <item>4) Additions: 6.38.3.1, 3.2, 4.1, 5.1, 6.1, 7.1</item>
                                        <item>5) SS. 6.38.8cd, 17 cd , 23cd, 26cd, 27cd - the second
                                            half has different text.</item>
                                        <item>6) SS.6.38.28 ab - the first half has different
                                            text.</item>
                                    </list>
                                </note>
                                <note resp="Vandana Lele"> This adhyaya is numbered 47 in the
                                    vulgate and 44.9 in NAK 5-333 <list>
                                        <item>1) Missing verses: 6.47.2, 6.47.4cd, 6.47.11, 12,
                                            6.47.21ab, 22cd, 23ab, 29cd, 30ab 6.47.54ab, 6.47.65cd,
                                            68cd 6.47.73cd, 75cd, 76, 79ab </item>
                                        <item>2) Additions: 6.47.4a, 4b, 6.47.13a, 13b, 13c, 13d,
                                            13e, 13f, 13,g, 13h, 13i, 13j, 6.47.65a, 66a, 68a
                                            6.47.73a, 73b, 73c, 73d, 73e, 73f, 73g </item>
                                        <item>3) Special Notes: <list>
                                                <item>i) The text of 6.47.4a and 4b added by me is
                                                  intermingled with 6.47.4cd which is shown missing
                                                  by me.</item>
                                                <item>ii) 6.47.20cd - the second half verse has
                                                  different text.</item>
                                                <item> iii) 6.47.38 - the first half verse has
                                                  different text. </item>
                                                <item>iv) 6.47.43cd and 44ab - the text is
                                                  intermingled i.e. 43.cd has only a word whereas
                                                  44ab has rest of the text.</item>
                                                <item>v) The Letter-numerals given on the folios are
                                                  not noted by me in the transcription. </item>
                                            </list>
                                        </item>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.55.45">

                <div n="58" type="adhyāya" corresp="chapter 56 in K and H">
                    <milestone unit="folio" n="475v4a(100v4a)"/>
                    <!-- dscn3450  fol 475.jpg -->

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.58.1"> athāto mū<cb/>tradoṣapratiṣedham vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.58.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.58.2.i"> āmādhyaśanaśīlasya<metamark function="yati"
                            >,</metamark> kaphapittapradūṣitaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         srotobhir bbastim āga<lb n="5"/>mya mūtraṃ vyāpādayed atha || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.58.2.ii"> vivarṇṇam āvilan sāndraṃ kṛcchrād api <cb/>ca tad
                        bhavet |
                        <caesura/>
                         tato vegapratīghātād udāvarttena vāyunā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.58.3"> prapīḍyaśoṣyamāṇe tu<metamark function="yati"
                            >,</metamark> mūtrarogās tadudbhavāḥ <lb n="6"/>|
                        <caesura/>
                         vātakuṇḍalikāṣṭhīlā vātabastis tathaiva ca ||
                        <caesura/>
                         mūtrātītaḥ sajaṭharo<metamark function="yati">,</metamark> mūtrotsaṅgaḥ
                        kṣayas tathā | </l>

                        vājīkarāṇy api ca yojayituṃ yateta || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.64.81"> grāsāntaran nāma | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.64.81a">piṇḍā<gap reason="omitted" extent="11" unit="char"/>
                    </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.64.82cd">
                        <gap reason="omitted" extent="4" unit="char"/>ṣu visṛjed vamanīyadhūmāc
                            chvāsādiṣu<gap reason="omitted" extent="3" unit="char"/>viṣṭa<pb
                            n="411v"/>guṇāṃś ca lehān || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.64.83"> evam ete daśauṣadhakālā bhavanti || bhavati cātra || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.64.84"> visṛṣṭe viṇmūtre viśadakaraṇai | dehe ca sulaghau |
                        <caesura/>
                        <unclear>sū</unclear>dve rodgare hṛdi ca vimale vāte ca sarati |
                        <caesura/>
                         tathānnaśuddhāyā kla<lb n="2"/>maparisame <unclear>ktū</unclear>kṣau
                        śithile |
                        <caesura/>
                         prayadeyas tv āhāro bhavati | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.64.84a">
                        <gap reason="omitted" extent="2" unit="char"/>ṣaja<gap reason="omitted"
                            extent="3" unit="char"/><unclear>sātmra</unclear>kriyeti | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.63.84b"> bhagavān āha dhanvantariḥ || </l>
                    <p xml:id="SS.6.64.84x" ana="trailer"> uttare tantre svastharakṣaṇīyaṃ
                        dvāpañcāśattamaḥ kā<lb n="3"/>yacikitsāyām aṣṭāviṃśatitamaḥ ||</p>
